03327: <div class="small" data-i18n="desc_isolation" style="margin-top:10px;">
03328:           红灯预警 <b>⚠️ 假隔离(曝光不足)</b> 意味着你虽然把它加入了 Exact 匹配，但由于 Exact 组竞价过低，实际上流量还是全在自动/广泛里跑！此时必须去 Exact 组加价！<br/>
03329: <b>【深度隔离闭环】</b>：点击右上角导出，系统将自动生成包含 <b>新建 Exact</b> 和 <b>来源组精准否定 (Negative Exact)</b> 的批量上传表格。

04915: // 统一处理 Amazon 报表里的百分比字段："12.34%" => 0.1234，"0.1234" => 0.1234，"12.34" => 0.1234
04916: const parsePercent = (x) => {
04917:   if (typeof x === "number") {
04918:     if (!isFinite(x)) return 0;
04919:     return Math.abs(x) > 1 ? x / 100 : x;
04920:   }
04921:   if (x === null || x === undefined || x === "") return 0;
04922:   const raw = String(x).trim();
04923:   const n = safeNum(raw);
04924:   if (!isFinite(n)) return 0;
04925:   return raw.includes("%") || Math.abs(n) > 1 ? n / 100 : n;
04926: };
04927: 
04928: const parsePercentField = (x, field="generic", source="") => {
04929:   if(x===null||x===undefined||x==="")return {value:0,ambiguous:false};
04930:   const raw=String(x).trim(),n=safeNum(raw);if(!Number.isFinite(n))return {value:0,ambiguous:false};
04931:   const hasPct=raw.includes("%");if(hasPct)return {value:n/100,ambiguous:false};
04932:   const ratioFields=new Set(["ctr","cvr","acos","share","rate"]),adjustFields=new Set(["placementAdjustment"]);
04933:   if(adjustFields.has(field))return {value:Math.abs(n)>10?n/100:(Math.abs(n)>1?n/100:n),ambiguous:Math.abs(n)===1};
04934:   if(ratioFields.has(field)){
04935:     if(Math.abs(n)<1)return {value:n,ambiguous:false};
04936:     if(Math.abs(n)>1)return {value:n/100,ambiguous:false};
04937:     const warning={fileName:source||"",reportType:"PERCENT_FIELD",warning:`Ambiguous naked percent value 1 in ${field}`};AdsStore.importWarnings.push(warning);return {value:n/100,ambiguous:true};
04938:   }
04939:   return {value:Math.abs(n)>1?n/100:n,ambiguous:Math.abs(n)===1};
04940: };
04941: const parseMetric = (x, type = "number", field="generic", source="") => type === "percent" ? parsePercentField(x,field,source).value : safeNum(x);

05073: const toISODate = (d) => {
05074:   if (typeof d === "number" && isFinite(d)) { 
05075:     const dateObj = new Date(Math.round((d - 25569) * 86400000)); 
05076:     return `${dateObj.getUTCFullYear()}-${String(dateObj.getUTCMonth()+1).padStart(2,'0')}-${String(dateObj.getUTCDate()).padStart(2,'0')}`; 
05077:   }
05078:   const s = String(d || "").trim();
05079:   if (!s) return "";
05080:   const isoMatch = s.match(/^(\d{4})[-\/.](\d{1,2})[-\/.](\d{1,2})/);
05081:   if (isoMatch) return `${isoMatch[1]}-${isoMatch[2].padStart(2,'0')}-${isoMatch[3].padStart(2,'0')}`;
05082:   const euMatch = s.match(/^(\d{1,2})[-\/.](\d{1,2})[-\/.](\d{4})/);
05083:   if (euMatch) {
05084:       const p1 = parseInt(euMatch[1], 10), p2 = parseInt(euMatch[2], 10), y = parseInt(euMatch[3], 10);
05085:       let m = p1, day = p2; if (p1 > 12) { day = p1; m = p2; }
05086:       return `${y}-${String(m).padStart(2,'0')}-${String(day).padStart(2,'0')}`;
05087:   }
05088:   const dt = new Date(s); 
05089:   if (!isNaN(dt.getTime())) return `${dt.getFullYear()}-${String(dt.getMonth()+1).padStart(2,'0')}-${String(dt.getDate()).padStart(2,'0')}`;
05090:   return ""; 
05091: };
05092: 
05093: const levenshtein = (a, b) => {
05094:     if (a === b) return 0;
05095:     if (a.length > b.length) { let tmp = a; a = b; b = tmp; }
05096:     let al = a.length, bl = b.length;
05097:     if (al === 0) return bl;
05098:     let row = Array.from({length: al + 1}, (_, i) => i);
05099:     let res = 0;
05100:     for (let i = 1; i <= bl; i++) {
05101:         res = i;
05102:         let diag = i - 1;
05103:         for (let j = 1; j <= al; j++) {
05104:             let cost = a[j - 1] === b[i - 1] ? 0 : 1;
05105:             let nextDiag = row[j];
05106:             res = Math.min(res + 1, nextDiag + 1, diag + cost);
05107:             row[j - 1] = diag;
05108:             diag = nextDiag;
05109:         }
05110:         row[al] = res;
05111:     }
05112:     return res;
05113: };

05129: const processInChunks = async (items, processFn, chunkSize = PERF.NORMALIZE_CHUNK, progressFn = null) => {
05130:   const results = new Array(items.length);
05131:   const size = Math.max(250, chunkSize || PERF.NORMALIZE_CHUNK);

05133:     const end = Math.min(items.length, start + size);

05135:     if (progressFn) progressFn(end, items.length);

05137:   }

05475: const cleanHeader = (h) => String(h).replace(/^\uFEFF/, '').replace(/\s+/g, '').toLowerCase();
05476: 
05477: const getAdProductMeta = (code) => AMAZON_AD_PRODUCT_META[String(code || "SP").toUpperCase()] || AMAZON_AD_PRODUCT_META.SP;
05478: const getAdProductDisplayLabel = (code) => getAdProductMeta(code).label;
05479: const isSponsoredProductsCode = (code) => String(code || "SP").toUpperCase() === "SP";
05480: const isBulkAllowedAdProduct = (code) => Boolean(getAdProductMeta(code).bulkAllowed);
05481: const detectAttributionWindowFromHeader = (header = [], fallbackCode = "SP") => {
05482:   const joined = header.map(cleanHeaderCompact).join("|");
05483:   if (/14(day|天)|14d/.test(joined)) return 14;
05484:   if (/7(day|天)|7d/.test(joined)) return 7;
05485:   const advertiserType = $("advertiserType")?.value || "seller";
05486:   if (String(fallbackCode || "SP").toUpperCase() === "SP" && advertiserType === "vendor") return 14;
05487:   return getAdProductMeta(fallbackCode).defaultAttributionDays || 7;

05489: const buildReportSchemaAudit = (reportType, header = [], map = {}, rows = [], fileName = "") => {
05490:   const warnings = [];
05491:   const requiredByType = {
05492:     ADS_REPORT: ["date", "campaign", "impr", "clicks", "spend", "sales7d", "orders7d"],
05493:     BUSINESS_REPORT: ["asin", "sessions", "units", "sales"],
05494:     PLACEMENT_REPORT: ["campaign", "placement", "impr", "clicks", "spend"],
05495:     SQP_REPORT: ["query", "searchVolume", "imprShare", "clickShare", "purchShare"],
05496:     TRANSACTION_REPORT: ["postedAt", "type", "productSales", "sellingFees", "fbaFees", "total", "status"]
05497:   };
05498:   const required = requiredByType[reportType] || [];
05499:   const missing = required.filter(k => !map[k]);
05500:   if (missing.length) warnings.push(`Missing columns: ${missing.join(", ")}`);
05501:   const adProduct = map.adProductType || (reportType === "ADS_REPORT" ? detectAdProduct(header, rows, map.adProduct) : "");
05502:   const attributionWindowDays = reportType === "ADS_REPORT" || reportType === "PLACEMENT_REPORT" ? detectAttributionWindowFromHeader(header, adProduct || "SP") : null;
05503:   if (reportType === "ADS_REPORT" && adProduct !== "SP") warnings.push(`${getAdProductDisplayLabel(adProduct)} imported as analysis-only; SP Bulk export is blocked for this report type.`);
05504:   if (reportType === "SQP_REPORT") warnings.push("SQP is search funnel/share data; do not merge it as advertising search-term performance.");
05505:   if (reportType === "TRANSACTION_REPORT") warnings.push("Combined Transaction Report is indexed by Posted Date. Taxes and transfers are excluded from product economics; advertising service fees are reconciliation-only.");
05506:   if (reportType === "ADS_REPORT") warnings.push(map.searchTerm ? "Metric grain=Search Term" : map.targeting ? "Metric grain=Targeting" : "Metric grain=Campaign; do not sum with another grain for the same period.");
05507:   return { schemaVersion: APP_SCHEMA_VERSION, fileName, reportType, adProduct: adProduct || "", attributionWindowDays, rowCount: rows.length || 0, headerCount: header.length || 0, missing, warnings, createdAt: new Date().toISOString() };
05508: };
05509: const recordSchemaAudit = (audit) => {
05510:   if (!audit) return;
05511:   AdsStore.schemaAudits.push(audit);
05512:   (audit.warnings || []).forEach(w => AdsStore.importWarnings.push({ fileName: audit.fileName, reportType: audit.reportType, warning: w }));
05513:   const label = audit.reportType === "ADS_REPORT" && audit.adProduct ? `${audit.reportType}/${getAdProductDisplayLabel(audit.adProduct)}` : audit.reportType;
05514:   if (audit.missing?.length) log(`Schema Audit ${label}: missing ${audit.missing.join(", ")}`, "warn");
05515:   else log(`Schema Audit ${label}: OK · rows=${audit.rowCount.toLocaleString()}${audit.attributionWindowDays ? ` · attribution=${audit.attributionWindowDays}d` : ""}`, "good");
05516:   (audit.warnings || []).forEach(w => log(`Guardrail: ${w}`, "warn"));
05517: };

05519: const normalizeAdProductValue = (value) => {
05520:     const v = String(value || "").trim().toLowerCase();
05521:     if (!v) return "";
05522:     if (v.includes("sponsored display") || v === "sd" || v.includes("display ads") || v.includes("display")) return "SD";
05523:     if (v.includes("sponsored brand") || v === "sb" || v.includes("brand")) return "SB";
05524:     if (v.includes("sponsored product") || v === "sp" || v.includes("product")) return "SP";
05525:     return "";
05526: };

05528: const detectAdProduct = (headers, sampleRows = [], adProductCol = null) => {
05529:     if (adProductCol && sampleRows.length) {
05530:       for (const row of sampleRows.slice(0, 80)) {
05531:         const detected = normalizeAdProductValue(row?.[adProductCol]);
05532:         if (detected) return detected;
05533:       }
05534:     }
05535:     const joined = headers.map(cleanHeader).join("|");
05536:     if (joined.includes("viewableimpression") || joined.includes("vpm") || joined.includes("view-through") || joined.includes("viewthrough") || joined.includes("display")) return "SD";
05537:     if (joined.includes("ntb") || joined.includes("new-to-brand") || joined.includes("newtobrand") || joined.includes("brandimpression")) return "SB";
05538:     return "SP"; 
05539: };

05627:   }

05684: const normalizeRow = (raw, map, sourceFile) => {
05685:   if (!raw) return null; 
05686:   const impr = safeNum(raw[map.impr]);
05687:   const clicks = safeNum(raw[map.clicks]);
05688:   const spend = safeNum(raw[map.spend]); 
05689:   const sales = safeNum(raw[map.sales7d]);
05690:   const orders = safeNum(raw[map.orders7d]); 
05691:   const st = String(raw[map.searchTerm] ?? "").trim();
05692:   const acosVal = sales > 0 ? spend / sales : (spend > 0 ? Infinity : 0);
05693:   const rawAcos = map.acos ? parsePercent(raw[map.acos]) : acosVal;
05694:   const normalizedAcos = sales > 0 ? (rawAcos || acosVal) : (spend > 0 ? Infinity : 0);
05695:   const rawRoas = map.roas ? safeNum(raw[map.roas]) : (spend > 0 ? Math.max(0, sales) / spend : 0);
05696:   const normalizedRoas = spend > 0 ? Math.max(0, rawRoas || (sales / spend)) : 0;
05697: 
05698:   const adProduct = normalizeAdProductValue(map.adProduct ? raw[map.adProduct] : "") || map.adProductType || "SP";
05699:   const reportGranularity = map.searchTerm ? "searchTerm" : (map.targeting ? "targeting" : "campaign");
05700:   return {
05701:     sourceFile: intern(sourceFile), 
05702:     adProduct: intern(adProduct),
05703:     adProductLabel: intern(getAdProductDisplayLabel(adProduct)),
05704:     attributionWindowDays: map.attributionWindowDays || getAdProductMeta(adProduct).defaultAttributionDays || 7,
05705:     reportSchemaVersion: APP_SCHEMA_VERSION,
05706:     reportGranularity,
05707:     workspaceKey: intern(getWorkspaceKey()),
05708:     marketplace: intern(normalizeMarketplace(map.marketplace ? raw[map.marketplace] : getWorkspaceConfig().marketplace)),
05709:     accountName: intern(String(map.accountName ? raw[map.accountName] : getWorkspaceConfig().accountName).trim()),
05710:     date: intern(toISODate(raw[map.date])), 
05711:     portfolio: intern(String(raw[map.portfolio] ?? "").trim()), 
05712:     campaign: intern(String(raw[map.campaign] ?? "").trim()), 
05713:     adGroup: intern(String(raw[map.adGroup] ?? "").trim()), 
05714:     targeting: intern(String(raw[map.targeting] ?? "").trim()), 
05715:     matchType: intern(String(raw[map.matchType] ?? "").trim()), 
05716:     searchTerm: st, 
05717:     searchTermLower: st.toLowerCase(), 
05718:     searchTermRoot: searchTermToRoot(st),
05719:     advertisedAsin: intern(extractAsinFromText(map.advertisedAsin ? raw[map.advertisedAsin] : "") || ""),
05720:     advertisedSku: intern(String(map.advertisedSku ? raw[map.advertisedSku] : "").trim()),
05721:     purchasedAsin: intern(extractAsinFromText(map.purchasedAsin ? raw[map.purchasedAsin] : "") || ""),
05722:     purchasedSku: intern(String(map.purchasedSku ? raw[map.purchasedSku] : "").trim()),
05723:     advertisedSales: map.advertisedSales ? Math.max(0,safeNum(raw[map.advertisedSales])) : null,
05724:     advertisedUnits: map.advertisedUnits ? Math.max(0,safeNum(raw[map.advertisedUnits])) : null,
05725:     otherSkuSales: map.otherSkuSales ? Math.max(0,safeNum(raw[map.otherSkuSales])) : null,
05726:     otherSkuUnits: map.otherSkuUnits ? Math.max(0,safeNum(raw[map.otherSkuUnits])) : null,
05727:     currentBid: map.currentBid ? safeNum(raw[map.currentBid]) : null,
05728:     biddingStrategy: intern(String(map.biddingStrategy ? raw[map.biddingStrategy] : "").trim()),
05729:     topOfSearchAdjustment: map.topOfSearchAdjustment ? parsePercentField(raw[map.topOfSearchAdjustment],"placementAdjustment",sourceFile).value : null,
05730:     productPagesAdjustment: map.productPagesAdjustment ? parsePercentField(raw[map.productPagesAdjustment],"placementAdjustment",sourceFile).value : null,
05731:     restOfSearchAdjustment: map.restOfSearchAdjustment ? parsePercentField(raw[map.restOfSearchAdjustment],"placementAdjustment",sourceFile).value : null,
05732:     impr, clicks, spend, sales: Math.max(0, sales), orders,
05733:     units: map.units ? safeNum(raw[map.units]) : null,
05734:     ctr: map.ctr ? parsePercentField(raw[map.ctr],"ctr",sourceFile).value : (impr > 0 ? clicks / impr : 0), 
05735:     cpc: map.cpc ? safeNum(raw[map.cpc]) : (clicks > 0 ? spend / clicks : 0),

05800: const isASINLike = (s) => {
05801:   const x = String(s || "").trim(); 
05802:   if (!x || x.length < 10) return false; 
05803:   const candidates = x.match(/[A-Z0-9]{10}/ig); 
05804:   if (!candidates) return false;
05805:   for (const c of candidates) { if (/^[B0-9][A-Z0-9]{9}$/i.test(c) && /\d/.test(c)) return true; }
05806:   return /asin\s*=\s*[A-Z0-9]{10}/i.test(x) || /asin\s*:\s*[A-Z0-9]{10}/i.test(x);
05807: };

05824: const XLSX_WORKER_LIB = "https://cdn.sheetjs.com/xlsx-0.20.3/package/dist/xlsx.full.min.js";
05825: const repairWorksheetRange = (ws) => {
05826:   if (!ws) return ws;
05827:   let maxR = -1, maxC = -1;
05828:   const dense = Array.isArray(ws) ? ws : (Array.isArray(ws["!data"]) ? ws["!data"] : null);
05829:   if (dense) {
05830:     for (let r = 0; r < dense.length; r++) {
05831:       const row = dense[r]; if (!row) continue;
05832:       for (let c = row.length - 1; c >= 0; c--) {
05833:         if (row[c] !== undefined && row[c] !== null) { maxR = Math.max(maxR, r); maxC = Math.max(maxC, c); break; }
05834:       }
05835:     }
05836:   } else {
05837:     for (const key of Object.keys(ws)) {
05838:       if (key[0] === "!") continue;
05839:       const m = /^([A-Z]+)(\d+)$/.exec(key); if (!m) continue;
05840:       let c = 0; for (const ch of m[1]) c = c * 26 + ch.charCodeAt(0) - 64;
05841:       maxR = Math.max(maxR, Number(m[2]) - 1); maxC = Math.max(maxC, c - 1);
05842:     }
05843:   }
05844:   if (maxR >= 0 && maxC >= 0) {
05845:     const actual = XLSX.utils.encode_range({s:{r:0,c:0},e:{r:maxR,c:maxC}});
05846:     const current = String(ws["!ref"] || "");
05847:     let currentRange = null; try { currentRange = current ? XLSX.utils.decode_range(current) : null; } catch (_) {}
05848:     if (!currentRange || currentRange.e.r < maxR || currentRange.e.c < maxC) ws["!ref"] = actual;
05849:   }
05850:   return ws;
05851: };
05852: const parseXLSXMainThread = async (buffer, maxRows) => {
05853:   const wb=XLSX.read(new Uint8Array(buffer),{type:"array",cellDates:false,dense:true});
05854:   if(wb.SheetNames.length>AMAZON_BULK_LIMITS.MAX_WORKSHEETS) throw new Error(`Workbook has ${wb.SheetNames.length} sheets; limit is ${AMAZON_BULK_LIMITS.MAX_WORKSHEETS}`);
05855:   const sheets=[]; let remaining=maxRows;
05856:   for(const sheetName of wb.SheetNames){
05857:     if(remaining<=0) break;
05858:     const ws=repairWorksheetRange(wb.Sheets[sheetName]);
05859:     let rows=XLSX.utils.sheet_to_json(ws,{defval:"",raw:true,blankrows:false});
05860:     if (!rows.length && ws && ws["!ref"] && ws["!ref"] !== "A1") {
05861:       rows=XLSX.utils.sheet_to_json(ws,{defval:"",raw:true,blankrows:false,range:ws["!ref"]});
05862:     }
05863:     const originalRows=rows.length; if(rows.length>remaining) rows=rows.slice(0,remaining);
05864:     rows.forEach(row=>{row.__sheetName=sheetName;});
05865:     if(rows.length){sheets.push({sheetName,rows,originalRows,truncated:originalRows>rows.length});remaining-=rows.length;}
05866:     await yieldToBrowser();
05867:   }
05868:   return sheets;
05869: };

07437: const execSafeDelta = (current, previous) => {
07438:   const a=safeNum(current), b=safeNum(previous);
07439:   if (!Number.isFinite(a) || !Number.isFinite(b)) return null;
07440:   if (Math.abs(b) < 0.000001) return Math.abs(a) < 0.000001 ? 0 : null;
07441:   return (a-b)/Math.abs(b);
07442: };

07446:   return {text:`${value>=0?"+":""}${(value*100).toFixed(1)}%${currentLang==="zh"?" vs 前期":" vs prior"}`,cls:good?"good":bad?"bad":"neutral"};

07521:   else if(current.acos<=targetAcos&&current.contributionProfit>0&&safeNum(deltas.sales)>.05&&winners.length>=2){decision="scale",decisionClass="good",verdict=currentLang==="zh"?"可控增长":"Controlled Growth",nextMove=currentLang==="zh"?`优先放量 ${winners.length} 个盈利资产，其中 ${exactGaps.length} 个需要沉淀到 Exact；只增加有证据的预算。`:`Scale ${winners.length} profitable assets first; ${exactGaps.length} still need Exact isolation. 07522:   else if(current.acos<=targetAcos&&safeNum(deltas.sales)<-.1&&safeNum(deltas.clicks)<-.1){decision="traffic",decisionClass="warn",verdict=currentLang==="zh"?"效率合格但流量收缩":"Traffic Gap",nextMove=currentLang==="zh"?"利润和ACOS仍可控，但点击与销售下降。优先检查预算耗尽、竞价覆盖和核心词展示份额。":"Efficiency is controlled but clicks and sales are falling. 07524:   const selectedDimension=EXEC_OVERVIEW_STATE.breakdown,breakdown=execBuildBreakdown(decisionRows,selectedDimension,targetAcos,wasteThreshold);

07530: const execBucketKey = (date,granularity) => {
07531:   if(granularity!=="weekly")return date;

07534: const execTransactionSalesByBucket = (scope,mode) => {
07535:   const txMode=$("transactionStatusMode")?.value||"accrual",market=getWorkspaceConfig().marketplace,start=$("dateStart")?.value||scope?.start||"",end=$("dateEnd")?.value||scope?.end||"",map=new Map();

07537:   rows.forEach(r=>{const key=execBucketKey(r.date,mode);map.set(key,(map.get(key)||0)+safeNum(r.productSales));});
07538:   return {map,available:rows.length>0,rows:rows.length,statusMode:txMode,start,end};
07539: };
07540: const execTrendSeries = (rows,granularity="auto") => {

07545:   const mode=granularity==="auto"?(calendarDays>45?"weekly":"daily"):granularity,groups=groupBy(adRows.filter(r=>r.date),r=>execBucketKey(r.date,mode)),tx=execTransactionSalesByBucket({start:selectedStart,end:selectedEnd},mode),keys=new Set([...groups.keys(),...tx.map.keys()]);

07548:     const transactionSales=tx.map.has(bucket)?tx.map.get(bucket):null,totalSales=transactionSales!==null?transactionSales:(biz.available?biz.sales:null),totalSpend=mature.spend+pending.spend;
07549:     return {date:bucket,label:mode==="weekly"?`${bucket.slice(5)}周`:bucket.slice(5),...mature,pendingSpend:pending.spend,bizSales:biz.available?biz.sales:null,transactionSales,totalSales,tacos:totalSales!==null&&totalSales>0?totalSpend/totalSales:null};

07564: // Executive Overview: account-level KPI snapshot sourced only from the Amazon Combined Transaction Report.

07566: const execTransactionAggregate = rows => {
07567:   rows=Array.isArray(rows)?rows:[];
07568:   const order=rows.filter(r=>r.category==="ORDER"),refund=rows.filter(r=>r.category==="REFUND"),trade=rows.filter(r=>r.category==="ORDER"||r.category==="REFUND");
07569:   const sumField=(list,field)=>list.reduce((a,r)=>a+safeNum(typeof field==="function"?field(r):r?.[field]),0);
07570:   const sales=sumField(order,"productSales"),refunds=Math.max(0,-sumField(refund,"productSales")),netSales=sales-refunds;
07571:   const orderUnits=sumField(order,r=>Math.max(0,safeNum(r.quantity))),refundUnits=sumField(refund,r=>Math.max(0,safeNum(r.quantity))),netUnits=Math.max(0,orderUnits-refundUnits);
07572:   const orderIds=new Set(order.map(r=>r.orderId).filter(Boolean)),skus=new Set(rows.map(r=>r.sku).filter(Boolean));
07573:   const amazonFees=Math.max(0,-sumField(trade,r=>safeNum(r.sellingFees)+safeNum(r.fbaFees)+safeNum(r.promotionalRebates)+safeNum(r.otherTransactionFees)+safeNum(r.other)));
07574:   const advertising=Math.max(0,-sumField(rows.filter(r=>r.category==="ADVERTISING"),"total"));
07575:   const operatingSettlement=sumField(rows.filter(r=>r.category!=="TRANSFER"),"total");
07576:   const resolver=buildSkuAsinResolver(),skuUnits=new Map();
07577:   for(const r of trade){const sku=String(r.sku||"").trim().toUpperCase();if(!sku)continue;const x=skuUnits.get(sku)||{order:0,refund:0,merchant:0};if(r.category==="ORDER"){const u=Math.max(0,safeNum(r.quantity));x.order+=u;if(/fbm|mfn|merchant|seller/i.test(String(r.fulfillment||r.fulfillmentType||r.fulfillmentChannel||"")))x.merchant+=u;}else x.refund+=Math.max(0,safeNum(r.quantity));skuUnits.set(sku,x);}
07578:   let purchaseCost=0,fbmShippingCost=0,costMatchedOrderUnits=0;
07579:   for(const[sku,x]of skuUnits){const asin=resolver.get(sku)||"",cost=resolveProductCostRecord(sku,asin,AdsStore.currentContext||UnifiedDecisionEngine.context());if(!cost||safeNum(cost.landedCost)<=0)continue;costMatchedOrderUnits+=x.order;purchaseCost+=Math.max(0,x.order-x.refund)*safeNum(cost.landedCost);fbmShippingCost+=x.merchant*safeNum(cost.fbmShippingCost);}
07580:   const finalNetProfit=operatingSettlement-purchaseCost-fbmShippingCost,costCoverage=orderUnits>0?costMatchedOrderUnits/orderUnits:0;
07581:   return {rows:rows.length,sales,refunds,netSales,orderUnits,refundUnits,netUnits,orderCount:orderIds.size,skuCount:skus.size,amazonFees,advertising,operatingSettlement,purchaseCost,fbmShippingCost,finalNetProfit,costMatchedOrderUnits,costCoverage,finalNetMargin:netSales>0?finalNetProfit/netSales:0,aov:orderIds.size?sales/orderIds.size:0,refundRate:sales>0?refunds/sales:0,unitRefundRate:orderUnits>0?refundUnits/orderUnits:0,netRetention:sales>0?netSales/sales:0,feeRate:netSales>0?amazonFees/netSales:0,adRate:netSales>0?advertising/netSales:0,settlementRate:netSales>0?operatingSettlement/netSales:0};
07582: };
07583: const execTransactionKpiSnapshot = fallbackScope => {

07586:   const eligible=filterTransactionRowsByScope(all,{mode,market});

07591:   return {available:currentRows.length>0,current:execTransactionAggregate(currentRows),previous,start,end,prevStart,prevEnd,mode,market,rowCount:currentRows.length};

07695:     searchTerm: r => r.searchTerm || "(blank)", 
07696:     searchTermRoot: r => r.searchTermRoot || "(blank)", 
07697:     targeting: r => r.targeting || "(blank)", 
07698:     campaign: r => r.campaign || "(blank)", 
07699:     adGroup: r => r.adGroup || "(blank)",

07703: 
07704: const sortRank = (items) => {
07705:   const {key,dir}=rankSort,mul=dir==="asc"?1:-1;
07706:   items.sort((a,b)=>{let av=a?.[key],bv=b?.[key];if(typeof av==="string"||typeof bv==="string"){av=String(av??"").toLowerCase();bv=String(bv??"").toLowerCase();return av.localeCompare(bv)*mul;}av=Number.isFinite(av)?av:(av===Infinity?Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER:0);bv=Number.isFinite(bv)?bv:(bv===Infinity?Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER:0);return (av===bv?0:av>bv?1:-1)*mul;});
07707: };

07735: const getBidGovPriorMap = (rows,view) => {
07736:   const map=new Map();
07737:   for(const r of rows||[]){const bucket=getBidGovBucket(r,view);if(!map.has(bucket))map.set(bucket,[]);map.get(bucket).push(r);}
07738:   const out=new Map();
07739:   for(const [bucket,list] of map){const m=sumMetrics(list),mean=clamp(m.cvr||sumMetrics(rows).cvr||.05,.003,.35),strength=clamp(Math.round(Math.sqrt(Math.max(1,m.clicks))*2),18,55);out.set(bucket,{mean,strength,metrics:m});}
07740:   return out;
07741: };
07742: const getBidGovPosterior = (metrics,prior={mean:.05,strength:24}) => {
07743:   const clicks=Math.max(0,safeNum(metrics.clicks)),orders=Math.max(0,Math.min(clicks,safeNum(metrics.orders))),a=orders+prior.mean*prior.strength,b=Math.max(0,clicks-orders)+(1-prior.mean)*prior.strength,mean=a/Math.max(1,a+b),variance=(a*b)/Math.max(1,((a+b)**2)*(a+b+1)),sd=Math.sqrt(Math.max(0,variance)),z=1.645;
07744:   return {mean,lower:clamp(mean-z*sd,0,1),upper:clamp(mean+z*sd,0,1),priorMean:prior.mean,priorStrength:prior.strength};
07745: };
07746: const getBidGovConfidence = ({matureMetrics:m,pendingMetrics:p,activeDays,orderDays,posterior,targetCpa}) => {
07747:   const spendEvidenceBase=Number.isFinite(targetCpa)&&targetCpa>0?targetCpa:Math.max(5,safeNum(getRules()?.spendNeg)||30),expectedClicks=Math.max(8,1/Math.max(.005,posterior.priorMean)),clickScore=Math.min(30,m.clicks/expectedClicks*30),orderScore=Math.min(30,m.orders*10),dayScore=Math.min(15,activeDays/7*15)+Math.min(10,orderDays/3*10),spendScore=Math.min(15,m.spend/spendEvidenceBase*15),pendingShare=(m.spend+p.spend)>0?p.spend/(m.spend+p.spend):0,penalty=pendingShare>.5?12:pendingShare>.25?5:0;
07748:   return clamp(Math.round(clickScore+orderScore+dayScore+spendScore-penalty),0,100);
07749: };

13650:   const downloadBlob=(blob,filename)=>{

13654:   const cleanSheetName=name=>String(name||'Sheet').slice(0,31).replace(/[\\/?*\[\]:]/g,'_')||'Sheet';
13655:   const normalizeCell=v=>{
13656:     if(v===null||v===undefined||v===''||(typeof v==='number'&&!Number.isFinite(v)))return '';
13657:     if(v instanceof Date)return v.toISOString();
13658:     if(typeof v==='object'){try{return JSON.stringify(v);}catch(e){return String(v);}}
13659:     return v;
13660:   };
13661:   const exportViaSheetJS=(sheets,filename)=>{
13662:     if(!window.XLSX?.utils?.book_new)return false;
13663:     const wb=window.XLSX.utils.book_new();
13664:     for(const s of sheets){
13665:       const aoa=[(s.headers||[]).map(normalizeCell),...(s.dataRows||[]).map(row=>(row||[]).map(normalizeCell))];
13666:       const ws=window.XLSX.utils.aoa_to_sheet(aoa);
13667:       if(aoa.length&&aoa[0].length){ws['!autofilter']={ref:window.XLSX.utils.encode_range({s:{r:0,c:0},e:{r:Math.max(0,aoa.length-1),c:aoa[0].length-1}})};ws['!freeze']={xSplit:0,ySplit:1};}
13668:       const widths=(s.headers||[]).map((h,i)=>{let max=String(h??'').length;for(const row of (s.dataRows||[]).slice(0,2000))max=Math.max(max,String(normalizeCell(row?.[i])).length);return{wch:Math.min(50,Math.max(10,max+2))};});
13669:       ws['!cols']=widths;
13670:       window.XLSX.utils.book_append_sheet(wb,ws,cleanSheetName(s.sheetName));
13671:     }
13672:     window.XLSX.writeFile(wb,filename,{compression:true});
13673:     return true;
13674:   };
13675:   const exportViaExcelJS=async(sheets,filename)=>{
13676:     if(!window.ExcelJS?.Workbook)return false;
13677:     const wb=new window.ExcelJS.Workbook();wb.creator='Ads Operations Integrity OS';wb.created=new Date();
13678:     for(const s of sheets){
13679:       const ws=wb.addWorksheet(cleanSheetName(s.sheetName),{views:[{state:'frozen',ySplit:1}]});
13680:       const headers=(s.headers||[]).map(normalizeCell);const hr=ws.addRow(headers);hr.font={bold:true,color:{argb:'FFFFFFFF'}};hr.fill={type:'pattern',pattern:'solid',fgColor:{argb:'FF1F2937'}};hr.alignment={vertical:'middle'};
13681:       if(headers.length)ws.autoFilter={from:{row:1,column:1},to:{row:1,column:headers.length}};
13682:       for(const row of (s.dataRows||[]))ws.addRow((row||[]).map(normalizeCell));
13683:       ws.columns.forEach((col,i)=>{let max=String(headers[i]??'').length;col.eachCell({includeEmpty:false},cell=>{max=Math.max(max,String(cell.value??'').length);});col.width=Math.min(50,Math.max(10,max+2));});
13684:     }
13685:     const buffer=await wb.xlsx.writeBuffer();downloadBlob(new Blob([buffer],{type:'application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.spreadsheetml.sheet'}),filename);return true;
13686:   };
13687:   const csvEscape=v=>{const s=String(normalizeCell(v));return /[",\n\r]/.test(s)?`"${s.replace(/"/g,'""')}"`:s;};
13688:   const exportCsvFallback=(sheets,filename)=>{

13690:     const csv='\uFEFF'+parts.join('\r\n');downloadBlob(new Blob([csv],{type:'text/csv;charset=utf-8'}),filename.replace(/\.xlsx$/i,'_fallback.csv'));
13691:   };

14147: <script id="shopScopeUiV1">
14148: (() => {
14149:   'use strict';
14150:   const SHOPS = Object.freeze(['ALL','YTDBNS','YY','JJ']);
14151:   const SHOP_LABELS = Object.freeze({ALL:'全部店铺',YTDBNS:'YTDBNS 店铺',YY:'YY 店铺',JJ:'JJ 店铺'});
14152:   const STORAGE_KEY = 'lr_active_shop_scope';
14153:   const normalizeShop = value => {
14154:     const shop = String(value || '').trim().toUpperCase();
14155:     return SHOPS.includes(shop) ? shop : 'ALL';
14156:   };
14157:   const storage = {
14158:     get: () => { try { return localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY) || 'ALL'; } catch (_) { return 'ALL'; } },
14159:     set: value => { try { localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, value); } catch (_) {} }
14160:   };
14161:   let activeShop = normalizeShop(storage.get());
14162: 
14163:   const syncShopUi = shop => {
14164:     document.querySelectorAll('#privateCloudImportPanel [data-shop]').forEach(button => {
14165:       const selected = button.dataset.shop === shop;
14166:       button.classList.toggle('active', selected);
14167:       button.setAttribute('aria-pressed', selected ? 'true' : 'false');
14168:       button.setAttribute('aria-checked', selected ? 'true' : 'false');
14169:     });
14170:     const hint = document.getElementById('activeShopHint');
14171:     if (hint) hint.textContent = `当前：${shop} · ${SHOP_LABELS[shop]}`;
14172:     document.documentElement.dataset.activeShop = shop;
14173:   };
14174: 
14175:   const setActiveShop = (value, options = {}) => {
14176:     const next = normalizeShop(value);
14177:     const changed = next !== activeShop;
14178:     activeShop = next;
14179:     storage.set(next);
14180:     syncShopUi(next);
14181:     window.ACTIVE_SHOP = next;
14182:     if (changed || options.force) {
14183:       window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('lr:shop-change', {
14184:         detail: { shop: next, label: SHOP_LABELS[next], source: options.source || 'shop-selector' }
14185:       }));
14186:     }
14187:     if (!options.silent && changed) {
14188:       try {
14189:         if (typeof notify === 'function') notify(`分析店铺已切换为 ${next} · ${SHOP_LABELS[next]}`, 'good');
14190:       } catch (_) {}
14191:     }
14192:     return next;
14193:   };
14194: 
14195:   const mount = () => {
14196:     const panel = document.getElementById('privateCloudImportPanel');
14197:     const loadButton = document.getElementById('btnPrivateCloudImport');
14198:     const logoutButton = document.getElementById('btnPrivateCloudLogout');
14199:     const status = document.getElementById('privateCloudImportStatus');
14200:     if (!panel || !loadButton || !logoutButton || !status) return false;
14201:     if (panel.dataset.shopUiReady === '1') {
14202:       syncShopUi(activeShop);
14203:       return true;
14204:     }
14205: 
14206:     loadButton.textContent = '☁ 加载私有云数据';
14207:     logoutButton.textContent = '清除密码';
14208:     const shell = document.createElement('div');
14209:     shell.innerHTML = `
14210:       <div class="cloudPanelHeader">
14211:         <div class="cloudPanelIcon" aria-hidden="true">☁</div>
14212:         <div class="cloudPanelCopy">
14213:           <div class="cloudPanelTitle">私有云数据</div>
14214:           <div class="cloudPanelSub">选择分析店铺，再安全读取广告、交易与成本数据</div>
14215:         </div>
14216:         <span class="cloudProviderBadge">CLOUDFLARE</span>
14217:       </div>
14218:       <div class="shopScopeCard">
